# Random

```
Random rand = new Random();

//[0,1) double
a = rand.nextDouble();
//int
b = rand.nextInt();
//[0,1)float
c  = rand.nextFloat();
//boolean
d = rand.nextBoolean();
//[0,10)int
e = rand.nextInt(10)
```
